Company: Hippo, Inc.

Calendar year 2022


Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: Hippo, Inc.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 21106, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2022-12-12
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Wayne, Pennsylvania, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Hippo, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2022-12-12 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

The Sole Director confirmed that notice of the meeting was duly given or waived.
The Sole Director’s presence satisfied the quorum requirement, and the meeting proceeded as duly constituted under the Delaware General Corporation Law.
The Sole Director participated via communications equipment by means of which all persons participating in the meeting could hear each other, and such participation constituted presence in person at the meeting.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
This was the first Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors following incorporation of the Corporation in 2022; no prior annual meeting of the Board was held and no prior annual board minutes were presented for approval.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Sunny Isles, Florida; Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; Portland, Oregon and development from Serbia; Bosnia and Herzegovina; Tunisia, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued development of the Corporation’s software and service offerings.  The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2022: Stabilization and growth phase: improved application architecture, introduced social features, and strengthened infrastructure and data pipelines. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All software, data models, algorithms, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including notes payable and similar obligations that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 8,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

After reviewing the materials on file for the meeting, the Sole Director relied in good faith on information, opinions, reports, and statements—including presentations from officers of the Corporation—on matters reasonably believed to fall within such persons’ professional or expert competence, under Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed the Corporation’s product and data roadmap for 2023, including API reliability targets, merchant integration milestones, and fraud-prevention initiatives.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2022 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2023 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2023 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2022)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 12, 2022, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2022, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Executed by (Sole Director):
Derek E. Pappas
Date: 2022-12-12

Operating addendum (Exhibit B)
Hippo, Inc.
(Delaware corporation)

Purpose
This addendum supplements the Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of the Corporation for 2022 and is designated as Exhibit B for attachment to those minutes upon filing with the minute book.

Detailed accomplishments (2022)

- Led project management and coordinated development timelines
- Refactored and redesigned the application to improve performance and maintainability
- Implemented critical API updates aligned with product requirements
- Developed UI screens for products, collections, and deals
- Introduced social features including likes and comments
- Implemented CI/CD pipelines and testing infrastructure
- Enhanced scraping systems, improving data quality and coverage
- Decommissioned legacy Hadoop-based pipeline after infrastructure failure
- Avoided high-cost vendor lock-in and initiated transition to new data solutions

Other materials
To the extent referenced in the minutes, this addendum may also include or incorporate by reference supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams).

Hippo, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of Hippo, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article III, Section 13 of the Corporation’s Amended and Restated Bylaws (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 12, 2022 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2022 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article III, Section 13(b) of those Bylaws, written consents must be delivered to the Corporation within sixty (60) days of the earliest dated consent; delivery to the registered office, if used, must be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, as set forth in the Bylaws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 12, 2022, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

Operating addendum (Exhibit B)
Hippo, Inc.
(Delaware corporation)

Purpose
This addendum supplements the Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of the Corporation for 2023 and is designated as Exhibit B for attachment to those minutes upon filing with the minute book.

Detailed accomplishments (2023)

- Refactored the application to improve scalability, performance, and maintainability
- Developed and deployed notifications and video services
- Maintained and enhanced core backend with new features and bug fixes
- Migrated database from H2 to PostgreSQL for improved reliability
- Extended product lookup capabilities with URL-based support
- Improved codebase structure and overall system stability
- Built scalable scraping and data processing workflows in Python
- Reverse engineered external APIs to enrich product datasets
- Rebuilt and modernized the data processing pipeline
- Decommissioned legacy Hadoop infrastructure and simplified the tech stack
- Initiated development of distributed processing using Spark
- Rebuilt browser extension to align with updated platform requirements

Other materials
To the extent referenced in the minutes, this addendum may also include or incorporate by reference supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams).

RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 11, 2023 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2023 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article III, Section 13(b) of those Bylaws, written consents must be delivered to the Corporation within sixty (60) days of the earliest dated consent; delivery to the registered office, if used, must be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, as set forth in the Bylaws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 11, 2023, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information

Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2024-12-09
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Denver, NC, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Hippo, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2024-12-09 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

The Sole Director confirmed that notice of the meeting was duly given or waived.
With Derek E. Pappas present as the Sole Director, the Board had a quorum and lawfully convened to transact business under the Delaware General Corporation Law.
Remote participation was used for the Sole Director’s attendance; the means employed allowed contemporaneous hearing among participants and were treated as satisfying any applicable in-person presence requirement.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2023-12-11 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Thessaloniki, Greece; Valencia, Spain; Knoxville, TN; Belgrade, Serbia; Athens, Greece; Istanbul, Turkey; Birmingham, England; Hoegaarden, Belgium; Denver, North Carolina, USA and development from Serbia; Bosnia and Herzegovina; Tunisia, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued development of the Corporation’s software and service offerings.  The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2024: Rebuild and optimization phase: full system redesign, infrastructure simplification, and significant cost reduction with improved scalability. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All software, data models, algorithms, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including notes payable and similar obligations that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 8,160,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

The Sole Director recorded reliance, in good faith, on the financial and operational materials circulated or reviewed for this meeting and on statements from officers of the Corporation on matters reasonably treated as within such persons’ professional or expert competence, as permitted by Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed the Corporation’s product and data roadmap for 2025, including API reliability targets, merchant integration milestones, and fraud-prevention initiatives.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2024 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2025 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2025 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2024)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 09, 2024, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2024, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Executed by (Sole Director):
Derek E. Pappas
Date: 2024-12-09

Operating addendum (Exhibit B)
Hippo, Inc.
(Delaware corporation)

Purpose
This addendum supplements the Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of the Corporation for 2024 and is designated as Exhibit B for attachment to those minutes upon filing with the minute book.

Detailed accomplishments (2024)

- Rebuilt the application with a scalable and maintainable architecture
- Improved code quality, stability, and development velocity
- Simplified system architecture by removing unused components
- Integrated Apache Solr for scalable search capabilities
- Designed and implemented a new indexing pipeline
- Built and scaled data processing pipelines across all partitions
- Developed recommendation systems and product grouping features
- Generated product collections from external data sources
- Developed a new web platform and admin panel for product management
- Decommissioned distributed data pipelines and reduced infrastructure complexity
- Reduced cloud infrastructure footprint by 75%
- Improved overall system performance and reliability

Other materials
To the extent referenced in the minutes, this addendum may also include or incorporate by reference supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams).

Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of Hippo, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article III, Section 13 of the Corporation’s Amended and Restated Bylaws (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 09, 2024 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article III, Section 13(b) of those Bylaws, written consents must be delivered to the Corporation within sixty (60) days of the earliest dated consent; delivery to the registered office, if used, must be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, as set forth in the Bylaws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Hippo, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2025-12-08 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2024-12-09 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Denver, North Carolina, USA; Lantana, Florida, USA; Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA and development from Serbia; Bosnia and Herzegovina; Tunisia, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued development of the Corporation’s software and service offerings.  The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2025: Release and scaling phase: public launch, continued backend improvements, and scaling of data processing and search capabilities. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All software, data models, algorithms, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including notes payable and similar obligations that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 8,160,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

After reviewing the materials on file for the meeting, the Sole Director relied in good faith on information, opinions, reports, and statements—including presentations from officers of the Corporation—on matters reasonably believed to fall within such persons’ professional or expert competence, under Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed the Corporation’s product and data roadmap for 2026, including API reliability targets, merchant integration milestones, and fraud-prevention initiatives.

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2025 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2026 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2026 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2025)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 08, 2025, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2025, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.

Hippo, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of Hippo, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article III, Section 13 of the Corporation’s Amended and Restated Bylaws (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 08, 2025 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2025 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article III, Section 13(b) of those Bylaws, written consents must be delivered to the Corporation within sixty (60) days of the earliest dated consent; delivery to the registered office, if used, must be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, as set forth in the Bylaws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 08, 2025, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article III, Section 13 of the Corporation’s Amended and Restated Bylaws (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article III, Section 13(b) of those Bylaws, written consents must be delivered to the Corporation within sixty (60) days of the earliest dated consent; delivery to the registered office, if used, must be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, as set forth in the Bylaws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Calendar year 2022


Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: Ritual Growth, Inc.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 27616, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2022-12-13
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Wayne, Pennsylvania, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Ritual Growth, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2022-12-13 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

There were no additional directors and no absences. The Sole Director’s presence satisfied the quorum requirement, and the meeting proceeded as duly constituted under the Delaware General Corporation Law. The Sole Director acknowledged on the record that notice requirements were satisfied by proper notice or waiver.
Remote participation was used for the Sole Director’s attendance; the means employed allowed contemporaneous hearing among participants and were treated as satisfying any applicable in-person presence requirement.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
This was the first Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors following incorporation of the Corporation in 2022; no prior annual meeting of the Board was held and no prior annual board minutes were presented for approval.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Sunny Isles, Florida; Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; Portland, Oregon and development from Poland; Romania; Portugal, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued product development during the year, including API servers and services and web applications; the Corporation did not ship a separate consumer mobile application during the period summarized.  The Corporation continued to operate hardware and cloud infrastructure using hosting providers including DigitalOcean and Hetzner. The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2022: Continued delivery on the Corporation’s web stack and APIs with contractor teams in Poland, Romania, and Portugal. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All application code, APIs, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including convertible instruments and vendor payment terms that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 4,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

The Sole Director stated that, in approving the matters minuted here, he relied in good faith on officer-prepared financial and operational materials and on other information, opinions, reports, and statements reasonably believed reliable on subjects within the presenters’ expert or professional competence, consistent with Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed go-to-market and client delivery priorities for 2023, including mobile companion workstreams, partner channel commitments, and release scheduling for the Corporation’s core web stack.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2022 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2023 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2023 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Bank of America, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2022)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 13, 2022, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2022, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Signature:
Derek E. Pappas
Dated: December 13, 2022

(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: Ritual Growth, Inc.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 27616, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2023-12-12
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Thessaloniki, Greece, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Ritual Growth, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2023-12-12 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

There were no additional directors and no absences. With Derek E. Pappas present as the Sole Director, the Board had a quorum and lawfully convened to transact business under the Delaware General Corporation Law. The Sole Director acknowledged on the record that notice requirements were satisfied by proper notice or waiver.
The Sole Director participated via communications equipment by means of which all persons participating in the meeting could hear each other, and such participation constituted presence in person at the meeting.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2022-12-13 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; Knoxville, TN; Austin, TX; Palo Alto, California; Surrey, Canada; Belgrade, Serbia; Thessaloniki, Greece and development from Poland; Romania; Portugal, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued product development during the year, including API servers and services and web applications; the Corporation did not ship a separate consumer mobile application during the period summarized.  The Corporation continued to operate hardware and cloud infrastructure using hosting providers including DigitalOcean and Hetzner. The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2023: Ongoing web and API development with distributed contractors in Poland, Romania, and Portugal. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All application code, APIs, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including convertible instruments and vendor payment terms that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 4,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

The Sole Director stated that, in approving the matters minuted here, he relied in good faith on officer-prepared financial and operational materials and on other information, opinions, reports, and statements reasonably believed reliable on subjects within the presenters’ expert or professional competence, consistent with Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed go-to-market and client delivery priorities for 2024, including mobile companion workstreams, partner channel commitments, and release scheduling for the Corporation’s core web stack.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2023 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2024 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2024 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Bank of America, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2023)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 12, 2023, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2023, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Signature:
Derek E. Pappas
Dated: December 12, 2023

Ritual Growth, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of Ritual Growth, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article II, Section 9 of the By-Laws of Ritual Growth, Inc. (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 12, 2023 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2023 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article II, Section 9 of those By-Laws, delivery to the Corporation’s registered office shall be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, where that delivery method is used; prompt notice of action taken without a meeting is required when consent is less than unanimous among applicable stockholders, as described in the By-Laws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 12, 2023, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

I. Call to Order:
The Special Meeting of the Board of Directors of Ritual Growth, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 12:00 PM on 2024-12-10 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director of the Corporation.

II. Roll Call and Quorum:
Director Present: Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

The Sole Director’s presence satisfied the quorum requirement, and the meeting proceeded as duly constituted under the Delaware General Corporation Law. The Sole Director acknowledged on the record that notice requirements were satisfied by proper notice or waiver.

In taking the actions reflected in these minutes, the Sole Director relied in good faith on information, opinions, reports, and statements—including financial and operational materials prepared for this meeting and presentations from officers of the Corporation—as to matters the Sole Director reasonably believed were within such persons’ professional or expert competence, as contemplated by Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


IV. Adjournment:
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Derek E. Pappas
Dated: December 10, 2024

Ritual Growth, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of Ritual Growth, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article II, Section 9 of the By-Laws of Ritual Growth, Inc. (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 10, 2024 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2024 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article II, Section 9 of those By-Laws, delivery to the Corporation’s registered office shall be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, where that delivery method is used; prompt notice of action taken without a meeting is required when consent is less than unanimous among applicable stockholders, as described in the By-Laws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 10, 2024, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

Minutes of the Quarterly Governance Meeting - 2024 Q1
Ritual Growth, Inc.
(Board of Directors – DE corporation)

Meeting Details
Date of Meeting: 2024-04-02
Time of Meeting: 1:00 PM
Location of Meeting: Belgrade, Serbia, via digital communication
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.

I. Call to Order:
The Quarterly Governance Meeting of the Board of Directors of Ritual Growth, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2024-04-02 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director of the Corporation.

II. Roll Call and Quorum:
Director Present: Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

The Sole Director’s presence satisfied the quorum requirement, and the meeting proceeded as duly constituted under the Delaware General Corporation Law. The Sole Director confirmed that notice had been duly given or validly waived for this meeting.
The Sole Director joined the meeting by approved digital means, with audio contemporaneous among participants, and such attendance was recorded as present in person at the meeting for quorum purposes.

III. Business Review:
The Sole Director reviewed quarterly infrastructure stability and confirmed that all assets, including software and related intellectual property, created during the quarter in the development centers located in Poland; Romania; Portugal are properly titled to and are the exclusive property of the Corporation.

The Sole Director stated that, in approving the matters minuted here, he relied in good faith on officer-prepared financial and operational materials and on other information, opinions, reports, and statements reasonably believed reliable on subjects within the presenters’ expert or professional competence, consistent with Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


IV. Resolution:
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolution:

RESOLVED, that all web, API, and supporting infrastructure work completed during the quarter—and related intellectual property—is hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved as assets of the Corporation.



V. Adjournment:
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Signature:
Derek E. Pappas
Dated: April 02, 2024

Calendar year 2025


Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: Ritual Growth, Inc.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 27616, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2025-12-09
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Wayne, Pennsylvania, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Ritual Growth, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2025-12-09 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

There were no additional directors and no absences. The Sole Director’s presence satisfied the quorum requirement, and the meeting proceeded as duly constituted under the Delaware General Corporation Law. Notice for the meeting had been provided or waived as required, which the Sole Director confirmed for the record.
The Sole Director attended using remote communications by which each participant could hear the others, and treated that participation as presence in person where permitted by applicable law and the Corporation’s bylaws.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2024-12-10 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Denver, North Carolina, USA; Lantana, Florida, USA; Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA and development from Poland; Romania; Portugal, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued product development during the year, including API servers and services and web applications; the Corporation did not ship a separate consumer mobile application during the period summarized.  The Corporation continued to operate hardware and cloud infrastructure using hosting providers including DigitalOcean and Hetzner. The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2025: Continued web/API iteration with intern support and contractor teams in Poland, Romania, and Portugal. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All application code, APIs, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including convertible instruments and vendor payment terms that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 4,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

For the actions described herein, the Sole Director relied in good faith on materials and oral presentations furnished for the meeting—including financial and operating summaries from officers of the Corporation—and on other information, reports, and statements presented as to matters within the presenters’ professional or expert competence, within the meaning of Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed go-to-market and client delivery priorities for 2026, including mobile companion workstreams, partner channel commitments, and release scheduling for the Corporation’s core web stack.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2025 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2026 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2026 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Bank of America, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2025)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 09, 2025, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2025, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Signature:
Derek E. Pappas
Dated: December 09, 2025

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Ritual Growth, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2026-12-15 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

There were no additional directors and no absences. The Sole Director’s presence satisfied the quorum requirement, and the meeting proceeded as duly constituted under the Delaware General Corporation Law. The Sole Director confirmed that notice of the meeting was duly given or waived.
The Sole Director attended using remote communications by which each participant could hear the others, and treated that participation as presence in person where permitted by applicable law and the Corporation’s bylaws.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2025-12-09 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA and development from Poland; Romania; Portugal, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued product development during the year, including API servers and services and web applications; the Corporation did not ship a separate consumer mobile application during the period summarized.  The Corporation continued to operate hardware and cloud infrastructure using hosting providers including DigitalOcean and Hetzner. The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2026: Planning and build-out phase: system flow definition and initial data systems. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All application code, APIs, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including convertible instruments and vendor payment terms that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 4,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

For the actions described herein, the Sole Director relied in good faith on materials and oral presentations furnished for the meeting—including financial and operating summaries from officers of the Corporation—and on other information, reports, and statements presented as to matters within the presenters’ professional or expert competence, within the meaning of Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed go-to-market and client delivery priorities for 2027, including mobile companion workstreams, partner channel commitments, and release scheduling for the Corporation’s core web stack.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2026 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2027 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2027 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Bank of America, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.

Ritual Growth, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of Ritual Growth, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article II, Section 9 of the By-Laws of Ritual Growth, Inc. (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 15, 2026 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2026 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article II, Section 9 of those By-Laws, delivery to the Corporation’s registered office shall be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, where that delivery method is used; prompt notice of action taken without a meeting is required when consent is less than unanimous among applicable stockholders, as described in the By-Laws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 15, 2026, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

(DGCL §228)

The undersigned, being the stockholders of DATA RECORD SCIENCE, INC., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), holding not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize the following action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted, hereby adopt the following resolutions by written consent pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective as of the date set forth below.

Ratification of Annual Board Meeting
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 14, 2022 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including the approval of financial statements, the budget for the ensuing fiscal year, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Notice to Non-Consenting Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the Corporation is authorized and directed to provide prompt notice of the taking of the foregoing corporate action by written consent, to the extent required by applicable law, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation, and the Corporation’s bylaws.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws.

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 14, 2022, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

(the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2023-12-13 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

None

V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The President reported that the Corporation is operated principally as a Delaware patent holding company, holding patents and related rights without conducting commercial software engineering as an operating business. Corporate administration, outside counsel coordination, and portfolio maintenance were overseen from Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; Knoxville, TN; Austin, TX; Palo Alto, California; Surrey, Canada; Belgrade, Serbia; Thessaloniki, Greece; the Corporation did not maintain third-party product-development centers comparable to a commercial SaaS operator during the year. The Sole Director summarized patent annuity and prosecution updates, portfolio housekeeping, and counsel reporting for the year.  Patents, patent applications, and related intellectual property held for investment were reaffirmed as assets of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including legacy acquisition-related holdbacks and similar obligations that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 5,346,132 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $0.001 per share.

For the actions described herein, the Sole Director relied in good faith on materials and oral presentations furnished for the meeting—including financial and operating summaries from officers of the Corporation—and on other information, reports, and statements presented as to matters within the presenters’ professional or expert competence, within the meaning of Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed portfolio strategy for 2024, including claim scope reviews, continuation strategy, and coordination with outside patent counsel.

VII. Resolutions

RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2023 are hereby approved.

RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2024 is hereby approved.

Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Wells Fargo Bank, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.

Stockholders Absent:
None.

The Chairperson declared that a quorum of stockholders was present and that the meeting was duly constituted to transact business.
The Chairperson further confirmed that any stockholders participating remotely were able to hear and be heard contemporaneously and that the Corporation had reasonable means to verify that each such person was a stockholder or proxyholder entitled to vote at the meeting.

The Chairperson confirmed that an alphabetized list of the names of the stockholders of record entitled to vote at this meeting (or a certified extract of the stock ledger) as of the record date was produced and made available for inspection by stockholders at the meeting in accordance with the Corporation’s bylaws, and that proxies and votes received in accordance with the bylaws were accepted for shares entitled to vote in accordance with such proxies.

IV. Notice; Waiver
The Chairperson confirmed that this annual meeting was held in reliance on written waivers of notice for stockholders entitled to cast the votes required by applicable law and the Corporation’s bylaws, consistent with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the bylaws. Executed waivers of notice are to be filed with these minutes as Exhibit A following execution (or delivery, as applicable).

V. Reports
The Chairperson presented and summarized the Corporation’s operational and financial highlights for the fiscal year. Stockholders had a reasonable opportunity to ask questions regarding the Chairperson’s report.

VI. Election of Directors
The following resolution was presented and adopted by the stockholders by the requisite vote under the Corporation’s bylaws and applicable law:

Election of Director
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is hereby elected as a director of the Corporation, to serve until the next annual meeting of stockholders and until such director’s successor is duly elected and qualified.

Directors were elected by a plurality of the votes cast by the shares present in person or by proxy and entitled to vote.

VII. Shares Outstanding
The Chairperson noted for the record that the Corporation had 5,346,132 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $0.001 per share as of the date of the meeting.

VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business properly brought before the meeting, the meeting was adjourned.

Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228)

The undersigned, being the stockholders of DATA RECORD SCIENCE, INC., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), holding not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize the following action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted, hereby adopt the following resolutions by written consent pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective as of the date set forth below.

Ratification of Annual Board Meeting
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 13, 2023 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including the approval of financial statements, the budget for the ensuing fiscal year, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Notice to Non-Consenting Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the Corporation is authorized and directed to provide prompt notice of the taking of the foregoing corporate action by written consent, to the extent required by applicable law, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation, and the Corporation’s bylaws.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws.

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 13, 2023, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

(the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2024-12-11 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The President reported that the Corporation is operated principally as a Delaware patent holding company, holding patents and related rights without conducting commercial software engineering as an operating business. Corporate administration, outside counsel coordination, and portfolio maintenance were overseen from Thessaloniki, Greece; Valencia, Spain; Knoxville, TN; Belgrade, Serbia; Athens, Greece; Istanbul, Turkey; Birmingham, England; Hoegaarden, Belgium; Denver, North Carolina, USA; the Corporation did not maintain third-party product-development centers comparable to a commercial SaaS operator during the year. The Sole Director summarized patent annuity and prosecution updates, portfolio housekeeping, and counsel reporting for the year.  Patents, patent applications, and related intellectual property held for investment were reaffirmed as assets of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including legacy acquisition-related holdbacks and similar obligations that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 5,346,132 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $0.001 per share.

The Sole Director stated that, in approving the matters minuted here, he relied in good faith on officer-prepared financial and operational materials and on other information, opinions, reports, and statements reasonably believed reliable on subjects within the presenters’ expert or professional competence, consistent with Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed portfolio strategy for 2025, including claim scope reviews, continuation strategy, and coordination with outside patent counsel.

Approval of 2025 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2025 is hereby approved.

RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Wells Fargo Bank, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.
