Ratification of Annual Board Meeting
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 11, 2024 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including the approval of financial statements, the budget for the ensuing fiscal year, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Notice to Non-Consenting Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the Corporation is authorized and directed to provide prompt notice of the taking of the foregoing corporate action by written consent, to the extent required by applicable law, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation, and the Corporation’s bylaws.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws.

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 11, 2024, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Executed by (stockholders):

Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: DATA RECORD SCIENCE, INC.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 24165, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2025-12-10
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Wayne, Pennsylvania, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
Immediately following the Annual Meeting of Stockholders of the Corporation held on 2025-12-10 commencing at 1:00 PM, The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of DATA RECORD SCIENCE, INC. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2025-12-10 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

With Derek E. Pappas present as the Sole Director, the Board had a quorum and lawfully convened to transact business under the Delaware General Corporation Law.
Notice for the meeting had been provided or waived as required, which the Sole Director confirmed for the record.
Remote participation was used for the Sole Director’s attendance; the means employed allowed contemporaneous hearing among participants and were treated as satisfying any applicable in-person presence requirement.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2024-12-11 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The President reported that the Corporation is operated principally as a Delaware patent holding company, holding patents and related rights without conducting commercial software engineering as an operating business. Corporate administration, outside counsel coordination, and portfolio maintenance were overseen from Denver, North Carolina, USA; Lantana, Florida, USA; Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; the Corporation did not maintain third-party product-development centers comparable to a commercial SaaS operator during the year. The Sole Director summarized patent annuity and prosecution updates, portfolio housekeeping, and counsel reporting for the year.  Patents, patent applications, and related intellectual property held for investment were reaffirmed as assets of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including legacy acquisition-related holdbacks and similar obligations that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 5,346,132 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $0.001 per share.

After reviewing the materials on file for the meeting, the Sole Director relied in good faith on information, opinions, reports, and statements—including presentations from officers of the Corporation—on matters reasonably believed to fall within such persons’ professional or expert competence, under Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed portfolio strategy for 2026, including claim scope reviews, continuation strategy, and coordination with outside patent counsel.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2025 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2026 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2026 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Wells Fargo Bank, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Executed by: Derek E. Pappas
Date: 2025-12-10

Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: DATA RECORD SCIENCE, INC.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 24165, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2026-12-16
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Wayne, Pennsylvania, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
Immediately following the Annual Meeting of Stockholders of the Corporation held on 2026-12-16 commencing at 1:00 PM, The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of DATA RECORD SCIENCE, INC. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2026-12-16 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

With Derek E. Pappas present as the Sole Director, the Board had a quorum and lawfully convened to transact business under the Delaware General Corporation Law.
Notice for the meeting had been provided or waived as required, which the Sole Director confirmed for the record.
The Sole Director joined the meeting by approved digital means, with audio contemporaneous among participants, and such attendance was recorded as present in person at the meeting for quorum purposes.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2025-12-10 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The President reported that the Corporation is operated principally as a Delaware patent holding company, holding patents and related rights without conducting commercial software engineering as an operating business. Corporate administration, outside counsel coordination, and portfolio maintenance were overseen from Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; the Corporation did not maintain third-party product-development centers comparable to a commercial SaaS operator during the year. The Sole Director summarized patent annuity and prosecution updates, portfolio housekeeping, and counsel reporting for the year.  Patents, patent applications, and related intellectual property held for investment were reaffirmed as assets of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including legacy acquisition-related holdbacks and similar obligations that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 5,346,132 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $0.001 per share.

For the actions described herein, the Sole Director relied in good faith on materials and oral presentations furnished for the meeting—including financial and operating summaries from officers of the Corporation—and on other information, reports, and statements presented as to matters within the presenters’ professional or expert competence, within the meaning of Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed portfolio strategy for 2027, including claim scope reviews, continuation strategy, and coordination with outside patent counsel.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2026 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2027 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2027 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Wells Fargo Bank, N.A., and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Executed by: Derek E. Pappas
Date: 2026-12-16

The Chairperson presented and summarized the Corporation’s operational and financial highlights for the fiscal year. Stockholders had a reasonable opportunity to ask questions regarding the Chairperson’s report.

(DGCL §228)

The undersigned, being the stockholders of DATA RECORD SCIENCE, INC., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), holding not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize the following action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted, hereby adopt the following resolutions by written consent pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective as of the date set forth below.

Ratification of Annual Board Meeting
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 16, 2026 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including the approval of financial statements, the budget for the ensuing fiscal year, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Notice to Non-Consenting Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the Corporation is authorized and directed to provide prompt notice of the taking of the foregoing corporate action by written consent, to the extent required by applicable law, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation, and the Corporation’s bylaws.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws.

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 16, 2026, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Calendar year 2023


Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: TeamBoost.ai, Inc.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 23049, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2023-12-14
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Thessaloniki, Greece, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of TeamBoost.ai, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2023-12-14 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

Quorum being established by the attendance of the Sole Director, the meeting was duly organized for business under the Delaware General Corporation Law. The Sole Director confirmed that notice had been duly given or validly waived for this meeting.
The Sole Director attended using remote communications by which each participant could hear the others, and treated that participation as presence in person where permitted by applicable law and the Corporation’s bylaws.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
This was the first Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors following incorporation of the Corporation in 2023; no prior annual meeting of the Board was held and no prior annual board minutes were presented for approval.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; Knoxville, TN; Austin, TX; Palo Alto, California; Surrey, Canada; Belgrade, Serbia; Thessaloniki, Greece and development from Brazil; Nigeria; Portugal, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued product development during the year, including API servers and services, web applications, and mobile applications.  The Corporation continued to operate hardware and cloud infrastructure using hosting providers including DigitalOcean and Hetzner. The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2023: Initial development phase: core platform architecture, mobile app creation, and foundational features were established, with a private beta release. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All mobile clients, server-side services, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including SAFEs, convertible notes, and similar instruments that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 10,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

After reviewing the materials on file for the meeting, the Sole Director relied in good faith on information, opinions, reports, and statements—including presentations from officers of the Corporation—on matters reasonably believed to fall within such persons’ professional or expert competence, under Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed mobile product velocity and infrastructure scaling for 2024, including app-store release cadence, on-device performance budgets, and push-notification reliability targets.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2023 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2024 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2024 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at First Citizens Bank & Trust Company, and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2023)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 14, 2023, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2023, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Signed:
Derek E. Pappas

TeamBoost.ai, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of TeamBoost.ai, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article II, Section 9 of the By-Laws of TeamBoost.ai, Inc. (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 14, 2023 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2023 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article II, Section 9 of those By-Laws, delivery to the Corporation’s registered office shall be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, where that delivery method is used; prompt notice of action taken without a meeting is required when consent is less than unanimous among applicable stockholders, as described in the By-Laws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 14, 2023, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of TeamBoost.ai, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article II, Section 9 of the By-Laws of TeamBoost.ai, Inc. (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 12, 2024 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2024 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article II, Section 9 of those By-Laws, delivery to the Corporation’s registered office shall be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, where that delivery method is used; prompt notice of action taken without a meeting is required when consent is less than unanimous among applicable stockholders, as described in the By-Laws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 12, 2024, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

(Delaware corporation)

I. Meeting Information

Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Delaware General Corporation Law; statutory references in these minutes follow that domicile. Place (and, where applicable, remote participation) reflects where the meeting was conducted for the stated date and may differ from the principal address.
Date: 2025-12-11
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Wayne, Pennsylvania, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of TeamBoost.ai, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2025-12-11 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

Quorum being established by the attendance of the Sole Director, the meeting was duly organized for business under the Delaware General Corporation Law. The Sole Director acknowledged on the record that notice requirements were satisfied by proper notice or waiver.
Remote participation was used for the Sole Director’s attendance; the means employed allowed contemporaneous hearing among participants and were treated as satisfying any applicable in-person presence requirement.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2024-12-12 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Denver, North Carolina, USA; Lantana, Florida, USA; Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA and development from Brazil; Nigeria; Portugal, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized continued product development during the year, including API servers and services, web applications, and mobile applications.  The Corporation continued to operate hardware and cloud infrastructure using hosting providers including DigitalOcean and Hetzner. The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2025: Release and stabilization phase: public rollout, improved reliability through testing, and continued enhancement of core features and system performance. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All mobile clients, server-side services, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including SAFEs, convertible notes, and similar instruments that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 10,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

The Sole Director recorded reliance, in good faith, on the financial and operational materials circulated or reviewed for this meeting and on statements from officers of the Corporation on matters reasonably treated as within such persons’ professional or expert competence, as permitted by Section 141(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed mobile product velocity and infrastructure scaling for 2026, including app-store release cadence, on-device performance budgets, and push-notification reliability targets.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2025 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2026 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2026 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at First Citizens Bank & Trust Company, and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2025)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 11, 2025, adopting stockholder resolutions under DGCL §228 for the year 2025, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Signed:
Derek E. Pappas

Purpose

- Expanded automated test coverage across the platform
- Enhanced onboarding, organization management, and notifications services

- Enhanced the tasks service and related workflows

The Corporation continued to operate hardware and cloud infrastructure using hosting providers including DigitalOcean and Hetzner. The Corporation has 10,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

The Sole Director discussed mobile product velocity and infrastructure scaling for 2027, including app-store release cadence, on-device performance budgets, and push-notification reliability targets.

Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at First Citizens Bank & Trust Company, and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.

TeamBoost.ai, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(DGCL §228; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of TeamBoost.ai, Inc., a DE corporation (the "Corporation"), and holding all of the outstanding shares of the Corporation entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent of the stockholders pursuant to the Delaware General Corporation Law, effective without a meeting to the same extent as if adopted at a duly held meeting. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the Corporation’s certificate of incorporation does not prohibit stockholder action by written consent as contemplated hereby, including action by the holders of outstanding shares of capital stock having not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize or take such action at a meeting at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted.
The undersigned acknowledges that this consent is intended to comply with Article II, Section 9 of the By-Laws of TeamBoost.ai, Inc. (Action Without Meeting), as well as Section 228 of the DGCL.

Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 17, 2026 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2026 to the extent permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Delaware General Corporation Law and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. Under Article II, Section 9 of those By-Laws, delivery to the Corporation’s registered office shall be by hand or by certified or registered mail, return receipt requested, where that delivery method is used; prompt notice of action taken without a meeting is required when consent is less than unanimous among applicable stockholders, as described in the By-Laws. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 17, 2026, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

Calendar year 2023


Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Wyoming corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: Loki Sports Enterprises, Inc.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 24709, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Wyoming Business Corporation Act. Place identifies where the meeting was conducted for the stated date (including by approved remote means).
Date: 2023-12-16
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Thessaloniki, Greece, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Loki Sports Enterprises, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2023-12-16 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

With Derek E. Pappas present as the Sole Director, the Board had a quorum and lawfully convened to transact business under the Wyoming Business Corporation Act. The Sole Director confirmed that notice of the meeting was duly given or waived.
The Sole Director joined the meeting by approved digital means, with audio contemporaneous among participants, and such attendance was recorded as present in person at the meeting for quorum purposes.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
This was the first Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors following incorporation of the Corporation in 2023; no prior annual meeting of the Board was held and no prior annual board minutes were presented for approval.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA; Knoxville, TN; Austin, TX; Palo Alto, California; Surrey, Canada; Belgrade, Serbia; Thessaloniki, Greece and development from United States; Pakistan, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized sports-media and venue-integration work during the year, including coordination with domestic (United States) operations and hockey stick manufacturing run through Pakistan-based production partners, with inventory and quality oversight centralized through the Corporation.  The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2023: Foundation phase: international sourcing for field hockey manufacturing through a dedicated agent in Sialkot, Pakistan. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All sports-media software, venue-integration tooling, product designs, manufacturing specifications for hockey sticks produced through the Corporation’s supply chain, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including equipment financing and season-cycle receivables that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 10,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

For the resolutions adopted here, the Sole Director relied in good faith on materials furnished for the meeting and on oral and written presentations from officers, in each case on subjects treated as within such persons’ professional or expert competence, as contemplated by W.S. 1977 § 17-16-830 (Wyoming Business Corporation Act).


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed fan engagement, venue partnerships, and media integrations for 2024, including tournament-season logistics, rights-holder coordination, and in-venue mobile experiences.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2023 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2024 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2024 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Truist Bank, and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2023)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 16, 2023, adopting stockholder resolutions under W.S. 1977 § 17-16-704 for the year 2023, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Executed and agreed:
Derek E. Pappas
Date: 2023-12-16

Calendar year 2024


Minutes of the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors
(Wyoming corporation)

I. Meeting Information
Company Name: Loki Sports Enterprises, Inc.
Principal Address: 30 N Gould St Ste 24709, Sheridan, WY 82801
Address note: The principal address above is the Corporation’s designated notice and filing address on the corporate records. The Corporation is governed by the Wyoming Business Corporation Act. Place identifies where the meeting was conducted for the stated date (including by approved remote means).
Date: 2024-12-14
Time: 1:00 PM
Place: Denver, NC, via digital communication
Type of Meeting: Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Loki Sports Enterprises, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2024-12-14 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

Quorum being established by the attendance of the Sole Director, the meeting was duly organized for business under the Wyoming Business Corporation Act. The Sole Director confirmed that notice of the meeting was duly given or waived.
Remote participation was used for the Sole Director’s attendance; the means employed allowed contemporaneous hearing among participants and were treated as satisfying any applicable in-person presence requirement.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2023-12-16 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Thessaloniki, Greece; Valencia, Spain; Knoxville, TN; Belgrade, Serbia; Athens, Greece; Istanbul, Turkey; Birmingham, England; Hoegaarden, Belgium; Denver, North Carolina, USA and development from United States; Pakistan, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized sports-media and venue-integration work during the year, including coordination with domestic (United States) operations and hockey stick manufacturing run through Pakistan-based production partners, with inventory and quality oversight centralized through the Corporation.  The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2024: Strategic partnerships and logistics: executive networking in Europe and first major inbound shipment of outdoor field hockey sticks. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All sports-media software, venue-integration tooling, product designs, manufacturing specifications for hockey sticks produced through the Corporation’s supply chain, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including equipment financing and season-cycle receivables that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 10,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

The Sole Director stated that he relied in good faith on officer-prepared financial and operational materials and on other information reasonably believed reliable on matters within the presenters’ areas of competence, consistent with W.S. 1977 § 17-16-830 of the Wyoming Business Corporation Act.


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed fan engagement, venue partnerships, and media integrations for 2025, including tournament-season logistics, rights-holder coordination, and in-venue mobile experiences.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2024 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2025 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2025 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Truist Bank, and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2024)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 14, 2024, adopting stockholder resolutions under W.S. 1977 § 17-16-704 for the year 2024, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Executed and agreed:
Derek E. Pappas
Date: 2024-12-14

Loki Sports Enterprises, Inc.
Written Consent of Sole Stockholder
Action by Written Consent of Stockholders
(W.S. 1977 § 17-16-704; annual meeting of stockholders)

The undersigned, being the sole stockholder of Loki Sports Enterprises, Inc., a WY corporation (the "Corporation"), and constituting all shareholders entitled to vote on the following matters, hereby adopts the following resolutions by written consent without a meeting pursuant to W.S. 1977 § 17-16-704 and the Wyoming Business Corporation Act, to the same extent as if the resolutions were approved at a duly held shareholders’ meeting by the unanimous vote of all shares entitled to vote thereon. The undersigned directs that this consent be delivered to the Corporation for inclusion in the minutes or filing with the corporate records as required by law. The undersigned acknowledges that, to the best of the undersigned’s knowledge, the articles of incorporation do not prohibit shareholder action by written consent in the manner set forth herein.
Approval of Board Actions
RESOLVED, that all actions taken and resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors of the Corporation at the Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on December 14, 2024 (or as otherwise recorded in the minutes of such meeting), including but not limited to the approval of financial statements, budgets, officer actions, and banking authorizations, are hereby ratified, confirmed, and approved in all respects.

Annual Meeting of Stockholders
RESOLVED, that the matters set forth in this Written Consent, including ratification of the Board’s actions taken at the annual board meeting referenced above, constitute or supplement, as applicable, the business addressed for purposes of the annual meeting of stockholders for the year 2024 to the extent permitted by the Wyoming Business Corporation Act, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws of the Corporation, and the undersigned waives any requirement to convene a separate annual meeting of stockholders for such year solely to duplicate the matters resolved herein.

Written Consent Mechanics
This Written Consent is intended to be delivered to the Corporation and to become effective in accordance with the Wyoming Business Corporation Act and the Corporation’s bylaws, including any timing requirements applicable to the delivery of consents bearing dated signatures. The Corporation is authorized and directed to file this Written Consent with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation and to give any prompt notice required by applicable law, the certificate of incorporation, and the bylaws (to the extent applicable).

Effective Date
This Written Consent shall be effective as of December 14, 2024, and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the stockholders of the Corporation.

Stockholder Certification
Sole Stockholder:
Derek E. Pappas

Executed by:
Derek E. Pappas

II. Call to Order
The Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors of Loki Sports Enterprises, Inc. (the “Corporation”) was called to order at 1:00 PM on 2025-12-13 by Derek E. Pappas, acting as Sole Director, President, and Treasurer of the Corporation.

III. Roll Call and Quorum
Director Present:
Derek E. Pappas (Sole Director)

Director Absent:
None

The Sole Director being present, a quorum was present, and the meeting was duly constituted to transact business in accordance with the Wyoming Business Corporation Act. The Sole Director acknowledged on the record that notice requirements were satisfied by proper notice or waiver.
The Sole Director participated via communications equipment by means of which all persons participating in the meeting could hear each other, and such participation constituted presence in person at the meeting.

IV. Approval of Prior Minutes
The minutes of the prior Annual Meeting of the Board of Directors held on 2024-12-14 were reviewed and approved by the Sole Director.
V. Reports of Officers

President’s Report:
The Sole Director reported on the Corporation’s operational and engineering activities for the fiscal year, including centralized management of globally distributed development and the use of operational office location(s) during the fiscal year, with operations conducted from Denver, North Carolina, USA; Lantana, Florida, USA; Wayne, Pennsylvania, USA and development from United States; Pakistan, while confirming that management, oversight, and decision-making remained centralized and continuously recorded through the Corporation’s official records. The Sole Director summarized sports-media and venue-integration work during the year, including coordination with domestic (United States) operations and hockey stick manufacturing run through Pakistan-based production partners, with inventory and quality oversight centralized through the Corporation.  The President’s report included the following accomplishments summary for the calendar year 2025: Expansion and diversification: new partnerships in Europe and Africa, supply-chain optimization in Sialkot, U.S. market entry, and expanded transatlantic shipments to Berlin. A written addendum designated as Exhibit B for attachment to these minutes upon filing sets forth detailed accomplishments for the period covered by the President’s report, together with supplemental technical materials furnished for the meeting (including technical specifications, roadmaps, KPIs, and architecture diagrams) where applicable. All sports-media software, venue-integration tooling, product designs, manufacturing specifications for hockey sticks produced through the Corporation’s supply chain, and related intellectual property developed during the year were reaffirmed as the exclusive property of the Corporation.

Treasurer’s Report:
The Treasurer reported that the Corporation remains solvent and that certain outstanding obligations, including equipment financing and season-cycle receivables that remain contingent on a future liquidity event, the timing of which has not yet been determined. The Sole Director acknowledged the status of such obligations and confirmed continued oversight of these matters. Franchise taxes and registered agent fees are paid and current. The Corporation has 10,000,000 shares of common stock issued and outstanding at a par value of $.0001 per share.

In taking the actions reflected in these minutes, the Sole Director relied in good faith on information, opinions, reports, and statements—including financial and operational materials prepared for this meeting and presentations from officers of the Corporation—as to matters the Sole Director reasonably believed were within such persons’ professional or expert competence, as contemplated by W.S. 1977 § 17-16-830 (Wyoming Business Corporation Act; standards for directors and reliance on information from officers and others reasonably believed reliable in their areas of competence).


VI. Discussion Items
The Sole Director discussed fan engagement, venue partnerships, and media integrations for 2026, including tournament-season logistics, rights-holder coordination, and in-venue mobile experiences.

VII. Resolutions
Upon consideration, the Sole Director adopted the following resolutions:

Approval of Financial Reports
RESOLVED, that the financial statements for the fiscal year 2025 are hereby approved.

Approval of 2026 Budget
RESOLVED, that the operating, engineering, and marketing budget for the fiscal year 2026 is hereby approved.

Banking Authorization
RESOLVED, that Derek E. Pappas is authorized to open, maintain, and manage one or more corporate bank accounts in the name of the Corporation at Truist Bank, and any successor institution, and to act as the sole authorized signatory with full authority to execute all related documents.



Stockholder Written Consent (2025)
The Sole Director noted that the Written Consent of Sole Stockholder dated December 13, 2025, adopting stockholder resolutions under W.S. 1977 § 17-16-704 for the year 2025, will be filed with the minutes of the stockholders of the Corporation upon execution, to be designated Exhibit A upon filing.


VIII. Adjournment
There being no further business to come before the Board, the meeting was adjourned.

Executed and agreed:
Derek E. Pappas
Date: 2025-12-13
